Tags

handle()

handle(string  $path, string  $method = null) : mixed

Handle the routes and match them towards the request, dispatch them when a match is made. Each route handler may throw exceptions that may redirect to an internal route for error handling.

Several routes can match and if the routehandler does not break execution flow, the route matching will carry on. Only the last routehandler will get its return value returned further.

Parameters

string $path

the path to find a matching handler for.
string $method

the request method to match.

any()

any(null|string|array  $method, null|string|array  $rule, null|string|callable  $action) : \Anax\Route\class|array

Add a route with a request method, a path rule to match and an action as the callback. Adding several path rules (array) results in several routes being created.

Parameters

null|string|array $method

as a valid request method.
null|string|array $rule

path rule for this route.
null|string|callable $action

to implement a handler for the route.
